CREATE TABLE [tab_compound_process_parameter_mapping](

  [process_container_id] bigint NOT NULL, 

  [process_container_type] text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PROCESS', 

  [process_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [process_parameter_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [container_id] bigint NOT NULL, 

  [container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [container_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [parameter_name] text NOT NULL, 

  PRIMARY KEY([process_container_id], [process_container_type], [process_name], [process_parameter_name]), 

  FOREIGN KEY([process_container_id], [process_container_type], [process_name], [process_parameter_name]) REFERENCES [tab_container_parameters]([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [parameter_name]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [parameter_name]) REFERENCES [tab_container_parameters]([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [parameter_name]) ON UPDATE CASCADE);

DROP TABLE tab_event_changed_container_molecules; -- due to schema mismatch
CREATE TABLE [tab_event_changed_container_molecules](

  [event_id] bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, 

  [event_container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [event_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [container_id] bigint NOT NULL, 

  [container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [container_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [molecule] text NOT NULL, 

  [calculation_method] text NOT NULL, 

  [formula_rate] text NOT NULL, 

  [use_as_value] bigint DEFAULT 1, 

  [use_amount] bigint DEFAULT 0, 

  PRIMARY KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [molecule], [calculation_method]), 

  FOREIGN KEY([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) REFERENCES [tab_calculation_method_rates]([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [molecule]) REFERENCES [tab_container_molecules]([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [molecule]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) REFERENCES [tab_event_conditions]([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE);
CREATE INDEX [tab_event_changed_moleculescontainer_id]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_molecules]([container_id]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_calculation_method_ratestab_event_changed_molecules]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_molecules](

  [calculation_method], 

  [formula_rate]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_event_conditionstab_event_changed_container_molecules]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_molecules](

  [event_id], 

  [event_container_type], 

  [event_name], 

  [calculation_method]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_container_moleculestab_event_changed_molecules]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_molecules](

  [container_id], 

  [container_type], 

  [container_name], 

  [molecule]);
DROP TABLE tab_event_changed_container_parameters; -- due to schema mismatch
CREATE TABLE [tab_event_changed_container_parameters](

  [event_id] bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, 

  [event_container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [event_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [container_id] bigint NOT NULL, 

  [container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [container_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [parameter_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [calculation_method] text NOT NULL, 

  [formula_rate] text NOT NULL, 

  [use_as_value] bigint DEFAULT 1, 

  PRIMARY KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [parameter_name], [calculation_method]), 

  FOREIGN KEY([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) REFERENCES [tab_calculation_method_rates]([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [parameter_name]) REFERENCES [tab_container_parameters]([container_id], [container_type], [container_name], [parameter_name]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) REFERENCES [tab_event_conditions]([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE);

CREATE INDEX [tab_calculation_method_ratestab_event_changed_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_parameters](

  [calculation_method], 

  [formula_rate]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_event_conditionstab_event_changed_container_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_parameters](

  [event_id], 

  [event_container_type], 

  [event_name], 

  [calculation_method]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_container_parameterstab_event_changed_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_container_parameters](

  [container_id], 

  [container_type], 

  [container_name], 

  [parameter_name]);
DROP TABLE tab_event_changed_generic_molecules; -- due to schema mismatch
CREATE TABLE [tab_event_changed_generic_molecules](

  [event_id] bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, 

  [event_container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [event_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [path_id] bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES [tab_object_paths]([path_id]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  [molecule] text NOT NULL, 

  [calculation_method] text NOT NULL, 

  [formula_rate] text NOT NULL, 

  [use_as_value] bigint DEFAULT 1, 

  [use_amount] bigint DEFAULT 0, 

  PRIMARY KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [path_id], [molecule], [calculation_method]), 

  FOREIGN KEY([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) REFERENCES [tab_calculation_method_rates]([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) REFERENCES [tab_event_conditions]([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE);

CREATE INDEX [tab_calculation_method_ratestab_event_changed_generic_molecules]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_molecules](

  [calculation_method], 

  [formula_rate]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_object_pathstab_event_changed_generic_molecules]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_molecules]([path_id]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_event_conditionstab_event_changed_generic_molecules]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_molecules](

  [event_id], 

  [event_container_type], 

  [event_name], 

  [calculation_method]);
DROP TABLE tab_event_changed_generic_parameters; -- due to schema mismatch
CREATE TABLE [tab_event_changed_generic_parameters](

  [event_id] bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, 

  [event_container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [event_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [path_id] bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES [tab_object_paths]([path_id]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  [parameter_name] text NOT NULL REFERENCES [tab_parameters]([parameter_name]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  [calculation_method] text NOT NULL, 

  [formula_rate] text NOT NULL, 

  [use_as_value] bigint DEFAULT 1, 

  PRIMARY KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [path_id], [parameter_name], [calculation_method]), 

  FOREIGN KEY([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) REFERENCES [tab_calculation_method_rates]([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) REFERENCES [tab_event_conditions]([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE);

CREATE INDEX [tab_event_conditionstab_event_changed_generic_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_parameters](

  [event_id], 

  [event_container_type], 

  [event_name], 

  [calculation_method]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_parameterstab_event_changed_generic_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_parameters]([parameter_name]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_object_pathstab_event_changed_generic_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_parameters]([path_id]);
CREATE INDEX [tab_calculation_method_ratestab_event_changed_generic_parameters]

ON [tab_event_changed_generic_parameters](

  [calculation_method], 

  [formula_rate]);
DROP TABLE tab_event_conditions; -- due to schema mismatch
CREATE TABLE [tab_event_conditions](

  [event_id] bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT 0, 

  [event_container_type] text NOT NULL, 

  [event_name] text NOT NULL, 

  [calculation_method] text NOT NULL, 

  [formula_rate] text NOT NULL, 

  [is_one_time] bigint DEFAULT 1, 

  PRIMARY KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name], [calculation_method]), 

  FOREIGN KEY([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) REFERENCES [tab_calculation_method_rates]([calculation_method], [formula_rate]) ON UPDATE CASCADE, 

  FOREIGN KEY([event_id], [event_container_type], [event_name]) REFERENCES [tab_containers]([container_id], [container_type], [container_name]) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE);
